## apps/realtime-gateway/README.md
- `apps/realtime-gateway/README.md` ‚Äî WebSocket fan-out gateway. Stateless pods behind a sticky LB; state lives in Redis Pub/Sub (and Redis Streams for replay). Carries live auction bids, order-status pushes, MCC live dashboards. Scales to millions of concurrent sockets by adding pods ‚Äî no socket state on the pod. Auth = same JWT; tenant-scoped channels. **[P1]**

## apps/realtime-gateway/package.json
- `apps/realtime-gateway/package.json` ‚Äî realtime gateway **[P1]**

## apps/stream-processor/README.md
- `apps/stream-processor/README.md` ‚Äî Kafka (MSK) stream processors for high-volume async: notification fan-out, search indexing, analytics ETL, fraud signals, mandi ingestion. outbox-relay publishes to Kafka; these consume. Partitioned by tenant_id for ordered, parallel processing. Phase 2 (SQS is fine until ~10k msg/s). **[P2]**
